# Sermon Reference Map

A complete catalog of every sermon, teaching, and study in the repository — organized by Bible book and passage. Includes both the Romans series (primary manuscripts in the root folder) and the full archive (Other-Sermons/).

---

## How to Use This Map

- **By passage**: Find what's been preached on any Bible text
- **By subject**: Scan for topical coverage (evangelism, suffering, election, etc.)
- **Avoid repetition**: Check before reusing an illustration or cross-reference
- **Find source material**: Locate earlier treatments of a passage for reuse or revision

---

## Romans Series (Primary Manuscripts)

These are the current, polished sermon manuscripts for the "Night Is Far Gone" series.

| Passage | Title | File | Subject |
|---|---|---|---|
| Romans 1:1-2 (Psalm 22) | Prophecy and the Credentials of Christ *(raw draft)* | `Romans 1 - Psalm 22 (Prophecy raw draft).md` | Debate/voting intro; Psalm 22 fulfillment table (11 prophecies); double-entendre model of prophecy; temple genealogy records; Lamb's Book of Life; heaven/hell three-door joke; gospel | ✅ Adrian Rogers "108 OT refs" — verified: Sermon #2299 "Christ of the Old Testament," LWF. Exact: "at least 108 [prophecies] many of which He had no control over, if He were only a human being." ✅ R.A. Torrey corrected: "300 in his book" is false — Torrey's actual lists total ~61–79 (New Topical Textbook, 1897); "300" is unattributed popular apologetics. Body updated. ✅ "68%" stat corrected to 65% — closest documented figure from Rick Joyner, Morningstar Prophetic Newsletter Vol. 3 No. 2 (Bob Jones self-report). ✅ Prophecy table: "Bones not broken" corrected from Ps 22:17 → Ps 34:20 (John 19:36 cites Ps 34:20 directly). ⚠️ Remaining fulfillment citations need line-by-line ESV check before congregational printing. |
| Romans 1:1-17 | The Power of God for Salvation | `Romans 1a - The Power of God for Salvation.md` | Retrospective introduction to Romans (preached after series progressed); *doulos*/called/set apart (*aphōrismenos*/*Pharisaios* wordplay, Phil 3:5); Damascus road illustration (Paul with arrest warrants, knocked off horse, blinded — effectual calling doctrine); gospel defined: promised beforehand (Isa 53:5 quoted), in Scriptures, concerning a Person, human and divine; obedience of faith bookend (1:5 and 16:26, James on dead/demonic faith); Paul's three motivations — thankfulness (v.8), desire to strengthen/mutual encouragement (vv.11-12, Paul corrects himself), obligation as debt; thesis statement (1:16-17): "I am not ashamed" (shame as Rome's weapon, cross designed to humiliate); *dunamis*; "For Salvation" — three-tense salvation mapped across Romans chapter groups (1-3, 3-5, 6-8, 9-11, 12-16); "To Everyone Who Believes" — faith as empty hand, instrument not cause (Eph 2:8-9); "To the Jew First and Also to the Greek" — sets up Romans 9-11; "From Faith for Faith" — faith as beginning, middle, and end; Luther and the righteousness of God; Habakkuk 2:4 in Romans/Galatians/Hebrews (three emphases); Winslow quote on the tree of the cross; Rom 15:24 Paul's plan to use Rome as base for Spain; Japan people group prayer; no gospel-invitation close (ends with recapitulation and prayer) |
| Romans 1:18-32 | Without Excuse | `Romans 1b - Without Excuse.md` | Continues from 1a; two revelations (v.17 righteousness v. v.18 wrath — same verb, two objects); suppress = hold down by force (pushing truth underwater imagery); Ps 19:1-2 "heavens declare" quoted; general revelation: nuclear resonance (1% shift turns carbon to oxygen), solar system positioning; sister's professor ("the more she studies science, the more she believes there must be an all-powerful God"); general revelation condemns but does not save (missions imperative — Turkey/Paul's journeys/seven churches of Revelation/Nicaea/Chalcedon, yet <0.1% evangelical today); six-step downward spiral (vv.21-23): refused honor → ingratitude → futile thinking → darkened hearts → claimed wisdom → exchanged glory ("image of God to image of a bug" progression); Calvin "perpetual factory of idols" (Institutes I.xi.8); three-fold giving over: impurity (vv.24-25, worship failure precedes moral collapse), dishonorable passions (vv.26-27, mirror not window — "this passage is about *us* not *them*"), debased mind (vv.28-31, *adokimos* — tested and found worthless like a counterfeit coin); Paul's mid-indictment doxology "who is blessed forever! Amen" (v.25 — God's glory not diminished by rebellion); 21 sins in vice list (ordinary sins: gossip, boasting, disobedience to parents); v.32 approval of sin as deepest level (weakness vs. advocacy — sinning vs. redefining glory to accommodate the fall); "But now" (Rom 3:21) previewed as structural resolution to the indictment; Winslow allusion: "God grew the tree and nurtured the soldiers and forged the iron" (closing); Mt 5:21-22 anger = murder (seed/fruit); Rom 1:14 obligation, 2:1 self-condemnation of the judge, 3:19 every mouth stopped — cross-refs woven through; gospel close (cross, blood, righteousness freely given, "run to God not away from Him"); Turkey people group prayer (85M population, <0.1% evangelical, land of Paul's missionary journeys and seven churches of Revelation — gospel light "almost gone out," civilizations can fall as individuals do) |
| Romans 1:18-32 | The Fingerprints of God | `Romans 1c - The Fingerprints of God.md` | Continues from 1b; 17,000 people groups / 7,000+ unreached framing stat (Joshua Project); general revelation sufficient to condemn but not to save (missions imperative restated — "Creation condemns. Only the gospel saves. And the gospel must be carried by human feet to human ears."); anthropic principle named as framework for design evidence; nuclear resonance via William Lane Craig — MRI as pedagogical vehicle (spectrum fired into body, nuclei "dance," reflect signal back), resonance window so narrow physicists said it "looked designed," 1% shift turns all carbon to oxygen, carbon-based life ceases; electromagnetism constant — one part in a thousand stronger and sun self-destructs; electron path stability ("no straight lines in nature" teaching hook) — unstable paths produce radiation and heat (Hiroshima/Nagasaki reference); baryon (*barus*, Greek "heavy") and entropy-per-baryon ratio 1:10⁹ — shift prevents galaxy formation; sister's professor: "the more she studies science, the more she believes there must be an all-powerful God"; earth's position in Milky Way — deeper means Magellanic Cloud blocks observation, farther out means less protection from rogue planets; Kuiper Belt and planetary shield illustration; ancient philosophers Empedocles (four elements) and Anaximander (fire-wheel cosmology) — beach/wonder motif ("sit and marvel at things bigger than us"); Paley's watchmaker argument applied; Grand Canyon illustration — Colorado River vs. flood theory, underground reservoir holding 3x surface water; Calvin "perpetual factory for idols" (Institutes I.xi.8); space elevator joke ("I bet they don't fix the elevator music"); vice list as mirror not window (Matt 5:21-22 cross-ref on anger = murder, "I daresay there is not a single person in this room who hasn't been angry"); Octavius Winslow quote on Christ creating the tree and nurturing the soldiers ⚠️ (manuscript itself flags: "Verify exact wording and source before preaching"); Michael Shultz meditation expanding Winslow — soldiers as boys, tree weathering storms, nails forged from ore at foundation of world, cross planned from eternity past, "He planned the moment of your conversion — and the moment of your death — with equal precision and care"; closing rhetorical question connecting baryon precision to personal providence ("do you think there is anything in your life that escapes his notice?"); personal illustration — would you sacrifice your child for someone else's sin (names Wyley as his child; Dottie, Willie, Richard, Greg, John, Bob as congregants); OT cycle of failure: sacrificial system, judges, Israel demands Saul over God; God's new covenant through his Son; election ("considering what we put God's Son through... it is more amazing to me that he would choose any of us at all"); Kris Kristofferson "Why Me Lord?" lyrics read; John 6:44 drawing of the Father; "Christians are not perfect. Christians are just forgiven."; BFM Article 2A — God the Father (full text read); Balija of India people group prayer (2.5 million, frontier status, <0.1% Christian, Hindu traders — bangles/salt/pearls, add Jesus to idol collection rather than exchange, alcohol permitted despite non-low caste — unusual combination noted) |
| Romans 1:18-24+ | The Darkness We Chose | `Romans 1.md` / `Romans 1 (2024).md` | Two manuscripts spanning cult-teaching format (Romans 1.md) and expository-anthropic format (Romans 1 (2024).md); cult series context: Unitarian Universalism (locally prominent); radical reformation origins; Arius and *homoousios* — changed one letter to make Jesus "similar to" rather than "same as" God; Pelagianism repackaged; Abelardianism (denies trinity while denying full deity of Christ — internal incoherence); universal salvation critique (if all roads lead to heaven, Christ's death pointless); "Frank" illustration (truly evil man's universalist funeral encourages nephews/coworker to continue in sin); Eph 2:1,8 dead in trespasses; Gen 2:7 dirt-to-life analogy; Pascal's Wager applied to Unitarians; Zeph 1:15-18 day of wrath; pulsar illustration (star so big light takes 1,000 years to orbit, yet heavens are God's footstool — scale of God's wrath); Romans 1:18-20 read; suppress = hold down truth by force; general revelation: anthropic principle named; nuclear resonance (attributed to William Lane Craig ⚠️); resonance at 0.8 = only helium, at 1.2 = only first four elements, 1% increase = all carbon becomes oxygen; electromagnetism stronger by one part in a thousand = sun tears apart; electron orbital paths — deviation produces radiation and heat (Hiroshima/Nagasaki reference); baryon entropy ratio 1:10⁹ (galaxy formation); sister's professor quote; Milky Way positioning; Kuiper belt and planetary shield; Empedocles (four elements) and Heraclitus (fire-wheel cosmology); watchmaker analogy on beach; Grand Canyon as possible flood evidence (underground water body 3x surface water); Calvin "factory for idols" (Institutes I.xi.8); vice list vv.28-31 as mirror of scripture; Mt 5:21-22 anger = murder; Octavius Winslow quote on tree/soldiers/iron ⚠️; Michael Shultz expansion (soldiers as boys, tree weathering storms, nails forged from ore at foundation of world); BFM Article 2A God the Father; election; "Why Me Lord" lyrics (Kris Kristofferson ⚠️); Jn 6:44 drawing; meta-narrative/moral law written on hearts; house-of-blocks analogy for biblical authority; Balija of India people group prayer (nearly 2M, 0.01% evangelical, Hindu traders of bangles/salt/pearls) |
| Romans 2:1+ | Don't Miss Heaven by 18 Inches *(raw transcript)* | `Romans 2.1 - Don't Miss Heaven by 18 Inches.md` | Greek vocative "ὦ ἄνθρωπε" (emphatic emotional force); "Britney Spears effect" (celebrity hypocrisy damages gospel witness, esp. Muslim world); inward before outward conformity; Luther on Law driving to Gospel (paraphrase); Moses glowing (Exodus 34:29-35); seminary chapel story: 18 inches = brain to heart; seminary friend who walked away; Matthew 7:23; Grace the dog illustration; distinct from the Mt 23/Col 3/Eph 2 sermon |
| Romans 2:1-11 | The Darkness We Deny *(repaired draft)* | `Romans 2 mt 23 col 3 eph 2.md` | Dirty cup illustration (dishwasher cup with moldy bone inside — clean outside, rotten inside, had to be destroyed); dead cat illustration (pet died in house, mother tried Febreze/Lysol/Dolce & Gabbana perfume — nothing covers the stench of death); Mt 23:27-33 whitewashed tombs; Mt 23:33 "You serpents, you brood of vipers, how are you to escape being sentenced to hell?"; first-century Jewish leaders as mirrors of modern Christians — right label, correct theology, moral knowledge, education, but no internal transformation; rabbis imposed stricter rules on converts than they followed; swearing by temple vs. gold contradictions (Mt 23:16-22); Rom 2:1-11 read (full ESV); v.3 "Do you suppose… that you will escape the judgment of God?"; v.4 God's kindness meant to lead to repentance; storing up wrath; v.6 "He will render to each one according to his works"; Sunday/Monday anaphora — cursing, sexual immorality, self-worship; 1 Cor 11:4-5 head coverings; Col 3:1-3 set your minds on things above; Col 3:5-6 put to death earthly desires, which is idolatry, wrath coming; Eph 2:4-10 "But God, being rich in mercy… made us alive together with Christ" (ESV); Christ doesn't help hide sin — He resurrects spiritual corpses, gives new natures; kidnapping case (39 American children rescued from sexual slavery — conversation with Georgia pastor about God's justice ⚠️ unverified incident details); Mt 18:6 millstone; Jonathan Edwards "Sinners in the Hands of an Angry God" (1741) drawing from Heb 10:31 "It is a fearful thing to fall into the hands of the living God" (ESV); ⚠️ Barnabas Piper on Christian political homelessness — exact wording unverified (likely social media); modern idolatry: comfort, security, pleasure elevated above God; politics as functional religion; "Would it be easier for them to know your politics? | Romans 3:19-26 | God's Wrath (Parts 1 & 2) | `Romans 3 - wrath of God (final).md` / `Romans 3 - pt 2.md` | **Part 1 (Wrath):** John Owen quote "He that has slight thoughts of sin never had great thoughts of God"; toothpaste tube marital conflict illustration (repeated violation of expressed wishes parallels humanity's relationship with God); cancer surgeon parable (surgeon hated cancer after it killed his mother — hatred of disease as part of virtue, parallels God's holy hatred of sin); hurricane metaphor (God's wrath is personal, measured, fair — unlike impersonal natural disaster); archery/target illustration (archers at mountain base shooting at peak = God's glory — no arrow threatens the mark, Rom 3:23); telescope illustration (single square inch of dark sky revealed tens of millions of galaxies — God's limitlessness = wrath's limitlessness); opposing magnets analogy (God and sin actively repel); A.W. Pink "The wrath of God is the revulsion of His being against that which is the contradiction of His holiness" (*Attributes of God*); Isa 6:3 holy holy holy; 1 Jn 1:5 no darkness; Hab 1:13 purer eyes; Ps 5:4; Col 1:17 holds all things together; Jan Huss martyrdom (burned at stake, last words: "I fear neither death nor fire"); Germanicus (young Christian, wild beasts, pagans converted); John Fisher (beheaded by Henry VIII, crown of thorns quote); John Bunyan (12 years imprisoned for preaching, blind daughter, offered release if he'd stop — refused; three extended quotes from prison writings); Jesus in Gethsemane — the cup was God's wrath, not man's cruelty; *tetelestai* (Logos: farmer/artist/priest/servant/merchant meanings — "paid in full"); definite atonement argument (if all sins paid for yet some burn in hell, no justice); Col 3 hidden with Christ. **Part 2 (Romans 3:10-end):** Archery illustration repeated (nobody's arrow threatens the mark); *hamartia* = "to miss the mark"; Rom 3:23 as doorway to grace; God doesn't grade on a curve — measures against blazing holiness; garage fire pastoral conversation ("God wants to crush the sin from our lives"); Jeremy Camp "Holy fire burn away"; only Christ hit the mark — His righteousness imputed; Rom 3:3-4 "By no means!" — our unfaithfulness doesn't make Him unfaithful; A.W. Tozer "God never hurries" and divine foreknowledge quotes; T-shirt: "The most comforting fact I know is that God has already factored in my stupidity" (traced to Tozer); 2 Cor 12:9 grace sufficient in weakness; Special Olympics friend in wheelchair ("What have I really won if I beat people with the same limitations?"); Rom 3:20 law as mirror not ladder; Third Day/Mac Powell lyric "I'll give you my life, for it's all I have to give"; gospel presentation |

The sun shines as clearly in the darkest day"; 1689 LBCF 16.5 on God leaving children to temptations; Spurgeon "God is too good to be unkind… when we cannot trace His hand, we must trust His heart"; Christ died for ungodly/weak/sinners/enemies — not the lovely or worthy (5:6-8); John Flavel "He who spared not His own Son… must have had a great design of love"; cross = where infinite wrath and infinite love meet; hurricane of divine judgment bent Christ low so believers might stand tall; 1689 LBCF 11.1 on justification; Pilgrim's Progress — burden falls off at cross; courtroom gives way to throne room; joy in God Himself not merely His gifts (5:11) — fuels sanctification; A.W. | Romans 9:19-33 (Part 3) | Coffee With Three Witnesses | `Romans 9 Pt 3.md` | Three OT/NT voices testify to sovereign mercy; **Witness 1 — Hosea** (vv.25-26): Gomer's unfaithfulness; children named Lo-Ruhamah ("No Mercy") and Lo-Ammi ("Not My People") as judgment verdicts; wildfire illustration (scorched acres, small green patch survives by design not chance); Titanic illustration (2,000+ sailed, remnant survived in lifeboats — "numbers didn't save; the boat did"); Owen "The preservation of a remnant is the fruit of God's distinguishing grace; | Romans 10:1-13 | The Gospel That Reformed the World | `Romans 10.md` | Five Solas of the Reformation applied to salvation; four pillars: Sola Scriptura (Word sufficient, Christ center of every page — Luther "Scripture is the cradle wherein Christ lies"), Sola Gratia (grace as substitution not leniency, pursues like "cheetah after limping gazelle" — Thomas Watson "Grace does not find men worthy; it makes them so"), Sola Fide (faith not a work but end of working, surrender of boasting — Spurgeon "Faith is the silver channel through which the mercy of God flows" — Luther "the gate to paradise"), Solus Christus (Christ plus anything ruins everything — Mary, sacraments, works all idolatry if added — Thomas Brooks "Christ did not die to make men salvable, but to make salvation sure"); Soli Deo Gloria conclusion; Luther's journey from confession/penance to justification by faith; Luther nailing theses (1517) echoes Paul's pen in Romans 10; Eph 2:1-5 dead in trespasses; Isa 53:5 pierced for transgressions; Heb 7 saves to the uttermost; 1 Tim 2:5 one mediator; Jn 14:6 "I am the Truth"; Acts 4:12 no other name; Florence Chadwick swimming illustration (swam 15 hrs from Catalina Island, quit 1 mile from shore in fog — "If I could have seen the shore, I would have made it" — sin's fog blinds us, we need faith supplied by God); Olympic marksman illustration (grace hits its mark every time); Boston Tea Party illustration (grace overthrows sin); toddler in white clothes/mud (salvation depends on Christ's grip not ours); Tim Keller "If your god never disagrees with you, you might just be worshipping an idealized version of yourself"; African spiritual closing "In the Morning When I Rise / Give Me Jesus"; Judah's historical error worshipping "queen of heaven" (Jeremiah); gospel |

| Romans 13:1-7 | Submission Before Sunrise | `Romans 13.md` | "Who Rules Our Rulers?" — 5-step staircase through Romans before exposition: Step 1 Problem (Rom 1-3 rebellion), Step 2 Solution (Rom 3:21-5 justification), Step 3 New Identity (Rom 6-8 freed from sin), Step 4 Assurance (Rom 9-11 God's plan doesn't wobble), Step 5 Ethic (Rom 12 living sacrifice in relationships); thesis: because our rulers are ruled by God, we live conscientiously — unless obedience to God requires disobedience to earthly rulers; I. The Reason: God Is Ultimate Authority (vv.1b-2) — every ruler answers to God whether they acknowledge Him or not; Paul wrote under Nero (hostile government, not Christian nation); resistance condemned = rebellious spirit that says "No one tells me what to do," not all civil disobedience; "A justified man can submit without panicking because he is not trying to save himself"; III. General Function of Government (vv.3-4) — guardrail metaphor (don't save your soul but restrain chaos); *diakonos* = instrument/tool, not savior or messiah; sword not borne in vain; "Christians are not anarchists"; IV. Practice: Pay What Is Owed (vv.6-7) — taxes, revenue, respect, honor; same respect whether "red or blue, Donkeys or Elephants"; don't sing loudly on Sunday and cheat quietly on Monday; clemency illustration (man served sentence with honor, granted clemency, later offended and lost rights — if justification depended on us we'd lose it; Christ maintains it); "Grace doesn't produce rebels. | Romans 16:1-27 | The Names in the Light | `Romans 16 - The Names in the Light.md` | Series finale; Phoebe (*diakonos*, *prostatis*) — letter carrier and patron (vv.1-2); Prisca and Aquila — risked their necks, church in their house, Prisca named first (vv.3-5); women who worked hard — Mary, Tryphaena, Tryphosa, Persis (*kopiaō* = labored to exhaustion) (vv.6,12); Rufus — likely son of Simon of Cyrene (Mk 15:21); Rufus's mother "a mother to me" (v.13); Tertius the scribe — one sentence of his own in someone else's letter (v.22); 26 names — slaves/freedmen, Jews/Gentiles, men/women; holy kiss (v.16); warning against divisive teachers — smooth talk and flattery, serve their own belly (*koilia*), deceive the naive (vv.17-20); Rom 14 (disputable matters) vs. Rom 16 (the doctrine) — confuse the two and you split the church or let wolves in; Genesis 3:15 echo — "God of peace will crush Satan under your feet" (v.20); doxology — "my gospel," *mystērion* hidden for long ages now disclosed, "obedience of faith" bookend (1:5 / 16:26), "to the only wise God be glory forevermore" (vv.25-27); Tunisian Arabs people group (12M, 99% Muslim, land of Tertullian/Cyprian/Augustine); series retrospective — midnight to dawn to daylight to names |

### Doctrines of Grace Series

A four-part series working through the scriptural foundations of the doctrines of grace (Total Depravity, Unconditional Election, Definite Atonement, Perseverance of the Saints). The first three sermons are not separately catalogued under this series heading in the archive; the fourth and final sermon has been polished to a primary manuscript.

|---|---|---|---|

When you are a believer, grace points to your need for the Law"; JD Greear's "fix my broken wanter" prayer; progressive sanctification — over time our wants come into line with God's; all of it starts with a relationship with Jesus; gospel close |

Part 1 — background on Israel's messianic expectations: sources: Josephus, 1 Maccabees, "The Jewish Messianic Expectation"; (a) wanted prosperity and earthly peace under the King of Peace — critiques prosperity-gospel TV preachers who promise earthly comfort in exchange for giving; (b) wanted a warrior-priest like Moses or Joshua — mediator, wise governor, formidable warrior, eternal king who would judge the dead and form a new world kingdom; Pharisees had created elaborate loopholes (e.g., Sabbath travel via tent sites) analogous to papal infallibility in Catholicism — man's word replacing God's word; Luke 23:18-19 — imprisoned for murder and insurrection; John: robber; Mark: murdering rebel; Josephus: a Sikario — the Sikarii were ≈4,000 assassins who attacked Roman and Jewish leaders claiming God's retribution, compared to modern al Qaeda; used God as a catchphrase to gain power (like a politician misquoting 1 John 2:4); Part 3 — Christ: Palm Sunday entry just one week prior (Hosanna = adoration/praise/joy); 400 years of prophetic silence before him; rode a donkey (sign of peace); healed, taught, sought and saved the lost; never sinned; Luke mentions his innocence 9 times; the parallel contrasts: Barabbas killed / Jesus raised the dead; Barabbas lied / Jesus brought life-saving truth; Barabbas built an earthly empire / Jesus pointed to the Father's eternal kingdom; Barabbas seized power by force / Jesus set aside his royal right and died on a cross for our glory and the Father's; Barabbas brought terror and death / Jesus brought joy, life everlasting, peace, hope, and a future; Application — Israel chose wrong because they were focused on desires and fears ("ME / MY stuff"); they wanted a warrior priest to free them from Rome and protect their kids, but they killed the only true source of hope, security, and protection; we do the same when self-focus displaces our relationship with Christ; Jesus bore the punishment Barabbas deserved — mercy, grace, second chance — just like us; closes with gospel call, Lord's Supper (1 Cor 11:23-26), Easter announcements (egg hunt, food pantry), Matt 11:28 benediction |
